<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a> (3875)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электрон.html>электро́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elektrón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elektrónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> electron, electronic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> lámpa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron tube; vacuum tube</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:луч.html>лу́ч</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnyj</b> lúč</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron beam</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:облако.html>о́блако</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnoje</b> óblako</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron cloud</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> púška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron gun</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нное</a></b> сродство́</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnoje</b> srodstvó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron affinity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:теория.html>тео́рия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> teórija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron theory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:физика.html>фи́зика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> fízika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electron physics</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:электронный.html>электро́нная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:формула.html>фо́рмула</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elektrónnaja</b> fórmula</i> ― <span class="e-translation">electronic formula</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***электроприбор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:электроприбор.html>электроприбо́р</a> (29729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">электро-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elektro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибор.html>прибо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pribór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электроприбор.html>электроприбо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elektropribór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электроприбор.html>электроприбо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электроприбор.html>электроприбо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:электроприбор.html>электроприбо́ров</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нт</a> (1886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elemént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>element, component</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry<span class="ib-comma">,</span> physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> element</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> person <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a specified type</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> element
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:консервативный.html>консервати́вные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нты</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщества</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">konservatívnyje <b>eleménty</b> óbščestva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the conservative element of society</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mužskój <b>elemént</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the male element (= men in general)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bad person, harmful person</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> electrochemical cell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гальванический.html>гальвани́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:элемент.html>элеме́нт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">galʹvaníčeskij <b>elemént</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/galvanic_cell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:galvanic cell">galvanic cell</a></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***элитарный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:элитарный.html>элита́рный</a> (23831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">elitario</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элитарный.html>элита́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elitárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> elite</li>
<li>elitist</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:элитный.html>эли́тный</a> (14765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элита.html>эли́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">elíta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элитный.html>эли́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">elítnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)эли́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)эли́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>elite</li>
<li>best, choice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:элитный.html>эли́тные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорта</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофе.html>ко́фе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elítnyje</b> sorta kófe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">choice coffees</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> luxury, luxurious
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:элитный.html>эли́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилой.html>жило́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>elítnyj</b> žilój dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">luxury residential building</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">best</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лучший.html>лу́чший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lúčšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отборный.html>отбо́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otbórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">luxury</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:элитарный.html>элита́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">elitárnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эмоция.html>эмо́ция</a> (4286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">émotion</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:энергетический.html>энергети́ческий</a> (6281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">énergét(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:энергетический.html>энергети́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">enɛrgetíčeskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> energy; energetic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:энергетический.html>энергети́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:напиток.html>напи́ток</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>enɛrgetíčeskij</b> napítok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">energy drink</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:энергетический.html>энергети́ческая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверхдержава.html>сверхдержа́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>enɛrgetíčeskaja</b> sverxderžáva</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>energy</b> superpower</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:энергетический.html>энергети́ческое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборудование.html>обору́дование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>enɛrgetíčeskoje</b> oborúdovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>power</b> equipment, <b>energy</b> equipment</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:энергия.html>эне́ргия</a> (1415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Energie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">energīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐνέργεια</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">enérgeia</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:энергия.html>эне́ргия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">enɛ́rgija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:энергия.html>эне́ргии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:энергия.html>эне́ргии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:энергия.html>эне́ргий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>energy, power</li>
<li>vitality</li>
<li>vigor</li></ol>
